runtime.Object) error\n   266→\n   267→// patcher breaks the process of patch application and retries into smaller\n   268→// pieces of functionality.\n   269→// TODO: Use builder pattern to construct  313→\tapplyPatchToCurrentObject(requextContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error)\n   314→\tcreateNewObject(requestContext context.Context) (runtime.Object, error)\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→type jsonPatcher struct {\n   318→\t*patcher\n   319→\n   320→\tfieldManager *managedfields.FieldManager\n   321→}\n   322→\n   323→func (p *jsonPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   324→\t// Encode will convert & return a versioned object in JSON.\n   325→\tcurrentObjJS, err := runtime.Encode(p.codec, currentObject)\n   326→\tif err != nil {\n   327→\t\treturn nil, err\n   328→\t}\n   329→\n   330→\t// Apply the patch.\n   331→\tpatchedObjJS, appliedStrictErrs, err := p.applyJSPatch(currentObjJS)\n   332→\tif err != nil {\n   333→\t\treturn nil, err\n   334→\t}\n   335→\n   336→\t// Construct the resulting typed, unversioned object.\n   337→\tobjToUpdate := p.restPatcher.New()\n   338→\tif err := runtime.DecodeInto(p.codec, patchedObjJS, objToUpdate); err != nil {\n   339→\t\tstrictError, isStrictError := runtime.AsStrictDecodingError(err)\n   340→\t\tswitch {\n   341→\t\tcase !isStrictError:\n   342→\t\t\t// disregard any appliedStrictErrs, because it's an incomplete\n   343→\t\t\t// list of strict errors given that we don't know what fields were\n   344→\t\t\t// unknown because DecodeInto failed. Non-strict errors trump in this case.\n   345→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n   346→\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), err.Error()),\n   347→\t\t\t})\n   348→\t\tcase p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn:\n   349→\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, append(appliedStrictErrs, strictError.Errors()...))\n   350→\t\tdefault:\n   351→\t\t\tstrictDecodingError := runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(append(appliedStrictErrs, strictError.Errors()...))\n   352→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n   353→\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), strictDecodingError.Error()),\n   354→\t\t\t})\n   355→\t\t}\n   356→\t} else if len(appliedStrictErrs) > 0 {\n   357→\t\tswitch {\n   358→\t\tcase p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn:\n   359→\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, appliedStrictErrs)\n   360→\t\tdefault:\n   361→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n   362→\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(appliedStrictErrs).Error()),\n   363→\t\t\t})\n   364→\t\t}\n   365→\t}\n   366→\n   367→\tif p.options == nil {\n   368→\t\t// Provide a more informative error for the crash that would\n   369→\t\t// happen on the next line\n   370→\t\tpanic(\"PatchOptions required but not provided\")\n   371→\t}\n   372→\tobjToUpdate = p.fieldManager.UpdateNoErrors(currentObject, objToUpdate, managerOrUserAgent(p.options.FieldManager, p.userAgent))\n   373→\treturn objToUpdate, nil\n   374→}\n   375→\n   376→func (p *jsonPatcher) createNewObject(_ context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   377→\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name)\n   378→}\n   379→\n   380→type jsonPatchOp struct {\n   381→\tOp    string      `json:\"op\"`\n   382→\tPath  string      `json:\"path\"`\n   383→\tFrom  string      `json:\"from\"`\n   384→\tValue interface{} `json:\"value\"`\n   385→}\n   386→\n   387→// applyJSPatch applies the patch. Input and output objects must both have\n   388→// the external version, since that is what the patch must have been constructed against.\n   389→func (p *jsonPatcher) applyJSPatch(versionedJS []byte) (patchedJS []byte, strictErrors []error, retErr error) {\n   390→\tswitch p.patchType {\n   391→\tcase types.JSONPatchType:\n   392→\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n   393→\t\t\tvar v []jsonPatchOp\n   394→\t\t\tvar err error\n   395→\t\t\tif strictErrors, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(p.patchBytes, &v); err != nil {\n   396→\t\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding patch: %v\", err))\n   397→\t\t\t}\n   398→\t\t\tfor i, e := range strictErrors {\n   399→\t\t\t\tstrictErrors[i] = fmt.Errorf(\"json patch %v\", e)\n   400→\t\t\t}\n   401→\t\t}\n   402→\n   403→\t\tpatchObj, err := jsonpatch.DecodePatch(p.patchBytes)\n   404→\t\tif err != nil {\n   405→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n   406→\t\t}\n   407→\t\tif len(patchObj) > maxJSONPatchOperations {\n   408→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewRequestEntityTooLargeError(\n   409→\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"The allowed maximum operations in a JSON patch is %d, got %d\",\n   410→\t\t\t\t\tmaxJSONPatchOperations, len(patchObj)))\n   411→\t\t}\n   412→\t\tpatchedJS, err := patchObj.Apply(versionedJS)\n   413→\t\tif err != nil {\n   414→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewGenericServerResponse(http.StatusUnprocessableEntity, \"\", schema.GroupResource{}, \"\", err.Error(), 0, false)\n   415→\t\t}\n   416→\t\treturn patchedJS, strictErrors, nil\n   417→\tcase types.MergePatchType:\n   418→\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n   419→\t\t\tv := map[string]interface{}{}\n   420→\t\t\tvar err error\n   421→\t\t\tstrictErrors, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(p.patchBytes, &v)\n   422→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   423→\t\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding patch: %v\", err))\n   424→\t\t\t}\n   425→\t\t}\n   426→\n   427→\t\tpatchedJS, retErr = jsonpatch.MergePatch(versionedJS, p.patchBytes)\n   428→\t\tif retErr == jsonpatch.ErrBadJSONPatch {\n   429→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(retErr.Error())\n   430→\t\t}\n   431→\t\treturn patchedJS, strictErrors, retErr\n   432→\tdefault:\n   433→\t\t// only here as a safety net - go-restful filters content-type\n   434→\t\treturn nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown Content-Type header for patch: %v\", p.patchType)\n   435→\t}\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→type smpPatcher struct {\n   439→\t*patcher\n   440→\n   441→\t// Schema\n   442→\tschemaReferenceObj runtime.Object\n   443→\tfieldManager       *managedfields.FieldManager\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→func (p *smpPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   447→\t// Since the patch is applied on versioned objects, we need to convert the\n   448→\t// current object to versioned representation first.\n   449→\tcurrentVersionedObject, err := p.unsafeConvertor.ConvertToVersion(currentObject, p.kind.GroupVersion())\n   450→\tif err != nil {\n   451→\t\treturn nil, err\n   452→\t}\n   453→\tversionedObjToUpdate, err := p.creater.New(p.kind)\n   454→\tif err != nil {\n   455→\t\treturn nil, err\n   456→\t}\n   457→\tif err := strategicPatchObject(requestContext, p.defaulter, currentVersionedObject, p.patchBytes, versionedObjToUpdate, p.schemaReferenceObj, p.validationDirective); err != nil {\n   458→\t\treturn nil, err\n   459→\t}\n   460→\t// Convert the object back to the hub version\n   461→\tnewObj, err := p.unsafeConvertor.ConvertToVersion(versionedObjToUpdate, p.hubGroupVersion)\n   462→\tif err != nil {\n   463→\t\treturn nil, err\n   464→\t}\n   465→\n   466→\tnewObj = p.fieldManager.UpdateNoErrors(currentObject, newObj, managerOrUserAgent(p.options.FieldManager, p.userAgent))\n   467→\treturn newObj, nil\n   468→}\n   469→\n   470→func (p *smpPatcher) createNewObject(_ context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   471→\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name)\n   472→}\n   473→\n   474→func newApplyPatcher(p *patcher, fieldManager *managedfields.FieldManager, unmarshalFn, unmarshalStrictFn func([]byte, interface{}) error) *applyPatcher {\n   475→\treturn &applyPatcher{\n   476→\t\tfieldManager: 485→\t}\n   486→}\n   487→\n   488→type applyPatcher struct {\n   489→\tpatch               []byte\n   490→\toptions             *metav1.PatchOptions\n   491→\tcreater             runtime.ObjectCreater\n   492→\tkind                schema.GroupVersionKind\n   493→\tfieldManager        *managedfields.FieldManager\n   494→\tuserAgent           string\n   495→\tvalidationDirective string\n   496→\tunmarshalFn         func(data []byte, v interface{}) error\n   497→\tunmarshalStrictFn   func(data []byte, v interface{}) error\n   498→}\n   499→\n   500→func (p *applyPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   501→\tforce := false\n   502→\tif p.options.Force != nil {\n   503→\t\tforce = *p.options.Force\n   504→\t}\n   505→\tif p.fieldManager == nil {\n   506→\t\tpanic(\"FieldManager must be installed to run apply\")\n   507→\t}\n   508→\n   509→\tpatchObj := &unstructured.Unstructured{Object: map[string]interface{}{}}\n   510→\tif err := p.unmarshalFn(p.patch, &patchObj.Object); err != nil {\n   511→\t\treturn nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding YAML: %v\", err))\n   512→\t}\n   513→\n   514→\tobj, err := p.fieldManager.Apply(obj, patchObj, p.options.FieldManager, force)\n   515→\tif err != nil {\n   516→\t\treturn obj, err\n   517→\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t// TODO: spawn something to track deciding whether a fieldValidation=Strict\n   520→\t// fatal error should return before an error from the apply operation\n   521→\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n   522→\t\tif err := p.unmarshalStrictFn(p.patch, &map[string]interface{}{}); err != nil {\n   523→\t\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict {\n   524→\t\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error strict decoding YAML: %v\", err))\n   525→\t\t\t}\n   526→\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, []error{err})\n   527→\t\t}\n   528→\t}\n   529→\treturn obj, nil\n   530→}\n   531→\n   532→func (p *applyPatcher) createNewObject(requestContext context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   533→\tobj, err := p.creater.New(p.kind)\n   534→\tif err != nil {\n   535→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create new object: %v\", err)\n   536→\t}\n   537→\treturn p.applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext, obj)\n   538→}\n   539→\n   540→// strategicPatchObject applies a strategic merge patch of `patchBytes` to\n   541→// `originalObject` and stores the result in `objToUpdate`.\n   542→// It additionally returns the map[string]interface{} representation of the\n   543→// `originalObject` and `patchBytes`.\n   544→// NOTE: Both `originalObject` and `objToUpdate` are supposed to be versioned.\n   545→func strategicPatchObject(\n   546→\trequestContext context.Context,\n   547→\tdefaulter runtime.ObjectDefaulter,\n   548→\toriginalObject runtime.Object,\n   549→\tpatchBytes []byte,\n   550→\tobjToUpdate runtime.Object,\n   551→\tschemaReferenceObj runtime.Object,\n   552→\tvalidationDirective string,\n   553→) error {\n   554→\toriginalObjMap, err := runtime.DefaultUnstructuredConverter.ToUnstructured(originalObject)\n   555→\tif err != nil {\n   556→\t\treturn err\n   557→\t}\n   558→\n   559→\tpatchMap := 562→\t\tstrictErrs, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(patchBytes, &patchMap)\n   563→\t\tif err != nil {\n   564→\t\t\treturn errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n   565→\t\t}\n   566→\t} else {\n   567→\t\tif err = kjson.UnmarshalCaseSensitivePreserveInts(patchBytes, &patchMap); err != nil {\n   568→\t\t\treturn errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n   569→\t\t}\n   570→\t}\n   571→\n   572→\tif 575→\treturn nil\n   576→}\n   577→\n   578→// applyPatch is called every time GuaranteedUpdate asks for the updated object,\n   579→// and is given the currently persisted object as input.\n   580→// TODO: rename this function because the name implies it is related to applyPatcher\n   581→func (p *patcher) applyPatch(ctx context.Context, _, currentObject runtime.Object) (objToUpdate runtime.Object, patchErr error) {\n   582→\t// Make sure we actually have a persisted currentObject\n   583→\ttracing.SpanFromContext(ctx).AddEvent(\"About to apply patch\")\n   584→\tcurrentObjectHasUID, err := hasUID(currentObject)\n   585→\tif err != nil {\n   586→\t\treturn nil, err\n   587→\t} else if !currentObjectHasUID {\n   588→\t\tobjToUpdate, patchErr = objToUpdateHasUID && !currentObjectHasUID {\n   602→\t\taccessor, err := meta.Accessor(objToUpdate)\n   603→\t\tif err != nil {\n   604→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   605→\t\t}\n   606→\t\treturn nil, errors.NewConflict(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name, fmt.Errorf(\"uid mismatch: the provided object specified uid %s, and no existing object was found\", accessor.GetUID()))\n   607→\t}\n   608→\n   609→\t// if this object supports namespace info\n   610→\tif objectMeta, err := meta.Accessor(objToUpdate); err == nil {\n   611→\t\t// ensure namespace on the object is correct, or error if a conflicting namespace was set in the object\n   612→\t\tif err := rest.EnsureObjectNamespaceMatchesRequestNamespace(rest.ExpectedNamespaceForResource(p.namespace, p.resource), objectMeta); err != nil {\n   613→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   614→\t\t}\n   615→\t}\n   616→\n   617→\tif err := checkName(objToUpdate, p.name, p.namespace, p.namer); err != nil {\n   618→\t\treturn nil, err\n   619→\t}\n   620→\treturn objToUpdate, nil\n   621→}\n   622→\n   623→func (p *patcher) admissionAttributes(ctx context.Context, updatedObject runtime.Object, currentObject runtime.Object, operation admission.Operation, operationOptions runtime.Object) admission.Attributes {\n   624→\tuserInfo, _ := request.UserFrom(ctx)\n   625→\treturn admission.NewAttributesRecord(updatedObject, currentObject, p.kind, p.namespace, p.name, p.resource, p.subresource, operation, operationOptions, p.dryRun, userInfo)\n   626→}\n   627→\n   628→// applyAdmission is called every time GuaranteedUpdate asks for the updated object,\n   629→// and is given the currently persisted object and the patched object as input.\n   630→// TODO: rename this function because the name implies it is related to applyPatcher\n   631→func (p *patcher) applyAdmission(ctx context.Context, patchedObject runtime.Object, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   632→\ttracing.SpanFromContext(ctx).AddEvent(\"About to check admission control\")\n   633→\tvar operation admission.Operation\n   634→\tvar options runtime.Object\n   635→\tif hasUID, err := hasUID(currentObject); err != nil {\n   636→\t\treturn nil, err\n   637→\t} else if !hasUID {\n   638→\t\toperation = admission.Create\n   639→\t\tcurrentObject = nil\n   640→\t\toptions = patchToCreateOptions(p.options)\n   641→\t} else {\n   642→\t\toperation = admission.Update\n   643→\t\toptions = patchToUpdateOptions(p.options)\n   644→\t}\n   645→\tif p.admissionCheck != nil && p.admissionCheck.Handles(operation) {\n   646→\t\tattributes := p.admissionAttributes(ctx, patchedObject, currentObject, operation, options)\n   647→\t\treturn patchedObject, p.admissionCheck.Admit(ctx, attributes, p.objectInterfaces)\n   648→\t}\n   649→\treturn patchedObject, nil\n   650→}\n   651→\n   652→// patchResource divides PatchResource for easier unit testing\n   653→func (p *patcher) patchResource(ctx context.Context, scope *RequestScope) (runtime.Object, bool, error) {\n   654→\tp.namespace = request.NamespaceValue(ctx)\n   655→\tswitch p.patchType {\n   656→\tcase types.JSONPatchType, types.MergePatchType:\n   657→\t\tp.mechanism = &jsonPatcher{\n   658→\t\t\tpatcher:      p,\n   659→\t\t\tfieldManager: scope.FieldManager,\n   660→\t\t}\n   661→\tcase types.StrategicMergePatchType:\n 671→\t// this case is unreachable if ServerSideApply is not enabled because we will have already rejected the content type\n   672→\tcase types.ApplyYAMLPatchType:\n   673→\t\tp.mechanism = newApplyPatcher(p, scope.FieldManager, yaml.Unmarshal, yaml.UnmarshalStrict)\n   674→\t\tp.forceAllowCreate = true\n   675→\tcase types.ApplyCBORPatchType:\n   676→\t\tif this point unless the feature gate is enabled.\")\n   678→\t\t\treturn nil, false, fmt.Errorf(\"%v: unimplemented patch type\", p.patchType)\n   679→\t\t}\n   680→\n   681→\t\t// The strict and non-strict funcs are the same here because any CBOR map with\n   682→\t\t// duplicate keys is invalid and always rejected outright regardless of strictness\n   683→\t\t// mode, and unknown field type\", p.patchType)\n   690→\t}\n   691→\tdedupOwnerReferencesTransformer := func(_ context.Context, obj, _ runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   692→\t\t// Dedup owner references after mutating admission happens\n   693→\t\tdedupOwnerReferencesAndAddWarning(obj, ctx, true)\n   694→\t\treturn obj, nil\n   695→\t}\n   696→\n   697→\ttransformers := []rest.TransformFunc{p.applyPatch, wasn't committed to storage because it's serialized size was too large,\n   712→\t\t// it is safe to remove managedFields (which can be large) and try again.\n   713→\t\tif isTooLargeError(err) && 719→\t\t\t\t\tfunc(_ context.Context, obj, _ runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n   720→\t\t\t\t\t\taccessor, _ := meta.Accessor(obj)\n   721→\t\t\t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n   722→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn obj, nil\n   723→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   724→\t\t\t\tresult, err = requestFunc()\n   725→\t\t\t}\n   726→\t\t}\n   727→\t\treturn result, err\n   728→\t})\n   729→\n   730→\t// In case 737→\treturn result, wasCreated, err\n   738→}\n   739→\n   740→// applyPatchToObject applies a strategic merge patch of <patchMap> to\n   741→// <originalMap> and stores the result in 746→\toriginalMap map[string]interface{},\n   747→\tpatchMap map[string]interface{},\n   748→\tobjToUpdate runtime.Object,\n   749→\tschemaReferenceObj runtime.Object,\n   750→\tstrictErrs []error,\n 755→\t\treturn interpretStrategicMergePatchError(err)\n   756→\t}\n   757→\n   758→\t// Rather than serialize the patched map to JSON, then decode it to an object, we go directly from a map to an 775→\t\t\tstrictDecodingError := runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(append(strictErrs, strictError.Errors()...))\n   776→\t\t\treturn errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n   777→\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", patchMap), strictDecodingError.Error()),\n   778→\t\t\t})\n   779→\t\t}\n   780→\t} else if len(strictErrs) > 0 {\n   781→\t\tswitch {\n   782→\t\tcase validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn:\n   783→\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, strictErrs)\n   784→\t\tdefault:\n   785→\t\t\treturn runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(strictErrs).Error()),\n   787→\t\t\t})\n   788→\t\t}\n   789→\t}\n   790→\n   791→\t// Decoding from JSON to a versioned object would apply defaults, so we do the same here\n   792→\tdefaulter.Default(objToUpdate)\n   793→\n   794→\treturn nil\n   795→}\n   796→\n   797→// interpretStrategicMergePatchError interprets the error type and returns an error with appropriate HTTP code.\n   798→func interpretStrategicMergePatchError(err error) error {\n   799→\tswitch err {\n   800→\tcase mergepatch.ErrBadJSONDoc, mergepatch.ErrBadPatchFormatForPrimitiveList, mergepatch.ErrBadPatchFormatForRetainKeys, mergepatch.ErrBadPatchFormatForSetElementOrderList, mergepatch.ErrUnsupportedStrategicMergePatchFormat:\n   801→\t\treturn errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n   802→\tcase mergepatch.ErrNoListOfLists, mergepatch.ErrPatchContentNotMatchRetainKeys:\n   803→\t\treturn errors.NewGenericServerResponse(http.StatusUnprocessableEntity, \"\", schema.GroupResource{}, \"\", err.Error(), 0, false)\n   804→\tdefault:\n   805→\t\treturn err\n   806→\t}\n   807→}\n   808→\n   809→// patchToUpdateOptions creates an UpdateOptions with the same field values as the provided PatchOptions.\n   810→func patchToUpdateOptions(po *metav1.PatchOptions) *metav1.UpdateOptions {\n   811→\tif po == nil {\n   812→\t\treturn nil\n   813→\t}\n   814→\tuo := &metav1.UpdateOptions{\n   815→\t\tDryRun:          po.DryRun,\n   816→\t\tFieldManager:    po.FieldManager,\n 825→\tif po == nil {\n   826→\t\treturn nil\n   827→\t}\n   828→\tco := &metav1.CreateOptions{\n   829→\t\tDryRun:          po.DryRun,\n   830→\t\tFieldManager:    po.FieldManager,\n PatchResource returns a function that will handle a resource patch.\nfunc PatchResource(r rest.Patcher, scope *RequestScope, admit admission.Interface, patchTypes []string) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {\n\t\tctx := req.Context()\n\t\t// For performance tracking purposes.\n\t\tctx, span := tracing.Start(ctx, \"Patch\", traceFields(req)...)\n\t\treq = req.WithContext(ctx)\n\t\tdefer span.End(500 * time.Millisecond)\n\n\t\t// Do this first, otherwise name extraction can fail for unrecognized content types\n\t\t// {\n\t\t\tcontentType = contentType[:idx]\n\t\t}\n\t\tpatchType := types.PatchType(contentType)\n\n\t\t// Ensure the patchType is one we support\n\t\tif !sets.NewString(patchTypes...).Has(contentType) requestTimeoutUpperBound.\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, requestTimeoutUpperBound)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tctx = request.WithNamespace(ctx, namespace)\n\n\t\toutputMediaType, _, err := negotiation.NegotiateOutputMediaType(req, scope.Serializer, scope)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tscope.err(err, w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tpatchBytes, err := limitedReadBodyWithRecordMetric(ctx, req, scope.MaxRequestBodyBytes, scope.Resource.GroupResource(), requestmetrics.Patch)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"limitedReadBody failed\", attribute.Int(\"len\", len(patchBytes)), attribute.String(\"err\", err.Error()))\n\t\t\tscope.err(err, w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"limitedReadBody succeeded\", attribute.Int(\"len\", len(patchBytes)))\n\n\t\toptions := &metav1.PatchOptions{}\n\t\tif err := metainternalversionscheme.ParameterCodec.DecodeParameters(req.URL.Query(), scope.MetaGroupVersion, options); err != nil {\n\t\t\terr = errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n\t\t\tscope.err(err, w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif errs := validation.ValidatePatchOptions(options, patchType); len(errs) > 0 {\n\t\t\terr := errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{Group: metav1.GroupName, Kind: \"PatchOptions\"}, \"\", errs)\n\t\t\tscope.err(err, w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\toptions.TypeMeta.SetGroupVersionKind(metav1.SchemeGroupVersion.WithKind(\"PatchOptions\"))\n\n\t\tadmit = admission.WithAudit(admit)\n\n\t\taudit.LogRequestPatch(req.Context(), patchBytes)\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Recorded the audit event\")\n\n\t\tvar baseContentType string\n\t\tswitch patchType {\n\t\tcase types.ApplyYAMLPatchType:\n\t\t\tbaseContentType = runtime.ContentTypeYAML\n\t\tcase types.ApplyCBORPatchType:\n\t\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.CBORServingAndStorage) {\n\t\t\t\t// This request should have already been rejected by the\n\t\t\t\t// Content-Type allowlist check. Return 500 because assumptions are\n\t\t\t\t// already broken and the feature is not GA.\n\t\t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(req.Context(), nil, \"The patch content-type allowlist check should have made this unreachable.\")\n\t\t\t\tscope.err(errors.NewInternalError(errors.NewInternalError(fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected patch type: %v\", patchType))), w, req)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tbaseContentType = runtime.ContentTypeCBOR\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tbaseContentType = runtime.ContentTypeJSON\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ts, ok := runtime.SerializerInfoForMediaType(scope.Serializer.SupportedMediaTypes(), baseContentType)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tscope.err(fmt.Errorf(\"no serializer defined for %v\", baseContentType), w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tgv := scope.Kind.GroupVersion()\n\n\t\tvalidationDirective := fieldValidation(options.FieldValidation)\n\t\tdecodeSerializer := s.Serializer\n\t\tif validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn || validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict {\n\t\t\tdecodeSerializer = s.StrictSerializer\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcodec := runtime.NewCodec(\n\t\t\tscope.Serializer.EncoderForVersion(s.Serializer, gv),\n\t\t\tscope.Serializer.DecoderToVersion(decodeSerializer, scope.HubGroupVersion),\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tuserInfo, _ := request.UserFrom(ctx)\n\t\tstaticCreateAttributes := admission.NewAttributesRecord(\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tscope.Kind,\n\t\t\tnamespace,\n\t\t\tname,\n\t\t\tscope.Resource,\n\t\t\tscope.Subresource,\n\t\t\tadmission.Create,\n\t\t\tpatchToCreateOptions(options),\n\t\t\tdryrun.IsDryRun(options.DryRun),\n\t\t\tuserInfo)\n\t\tstaticUpdateAttributes := admission.NewAttributesRecord(\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tnil,\n\t\t\tscope.Kind,\n\t\t\tnamespace,\n\t\t\tname,\n\t\t\tscope.Resource,\n\t\t\tscope.Subresource,\n\t\t\tadmission.Update,\n\t\t\tpatchToUpdateOptions(options),\n\t\t\tdryrun.IsDryRun(options.DryRun),\n\t\t\tuserInfo,\n\t\t)\n\n\t\tadmit = fieldmanager.NewManagedFieldsValidatingAdmissionController(admit)\n\n\t\tmutatingAdmission, _ := admit.(admission.MutationInterface)\n\t\tcreateAuthorizerAttributes := authorizer.AttributesRecord{\n\t\t\tUser:            userInfo,\n\t\t\tResourceRequest: true,\n\t\t\tPath:            req.URL.Path,\n\t\t\tVerb:            \"create\",\n\t\t\tAPIGroup:        scope.Resource.Group,\n\t\t\tAPIVersion:      scope.Resource.Version,\n\t\t\tResource:        scope.Resource.Resource,\n\t\t\tSubresource:     scope.Subresource,\n\t\t\tNamespace:       namespace,\n\t\t\tName:            name,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tp := patcher{\n\t\t\tnamer:               scope.Namer,\n\t\t\tcreater:             scope.Creater,\n\t\t\tdefaulter:           scope.Defaulter,\n\t\t\ttyper:               scope.Typer,\n\t\t\tunsafeConvertor:     scope.UnsafeConvertor,\n\t\t\tkind:                scope.Kind,\n\t\t\tresource:            scope.Resource,\n\t\t\tsubresource:         scope.Subresource,\n\t\t\tdryRun:              dryrun.IsDryRun(options.DryRun),\n\t\t\tvalidationDirective: validationDirective,\n\n\t\t\tobjectInterfaces: scope,\n\n\t\t\thubGroupVersion: scope.HubGroupVersion,\n\n\t\t\tcreateValidation: withAuthorization(rest.AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc(admit, staticCreateAttributes, scope), scope.Authorizer, createAuthorizerAttributes),\n\t\t\tupdateValidation: rest.AdmissionToValidateObjectUpdateFunc(admit, staticUpdateAttributes, scope),\n\t\t\tadmissionCheck:   mutatingAdmission,\n\n\t\t\tcodec: codec,\n\n\t\t\toptions: options,\n\n\t\t\trestPatcher: r,\n\t\t\tname:        name,\n\t\t\tpatchType:   patchType,\n\t\t\tpatchBytes:  patchBytes,\n\t\t\tuserAgent:   req.UserAgent(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresult, wasCreated, err := p.patchResource(ctx, scope)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tscope.err(err, w, req)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"Object stored in database\")\n\n\t\tstatus := http.StatusOK\n\t\tif wasCreated {\n\t\t\tstatus = http.StatusCreated\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tspan.AddEvent(\"About to write a response\")\n\t\tdefer span.AddEvent(\"Writing http response done\")\n\t\ttransformResponseObject(ctx, scope, req, w, status, outputMediaType, result)\n\t}\n}\n\ntype mutateObjectUpdateFunc func(ctx context.Context, obj, old runtime.Object) error\n\n// patcher breaks the process of patch application and retries into smaller\n// pieces of functionality.\n// TODO: Use builder pattern to construct this object?\n// TODO: As part of that effort, some aspects of PatchResource above could be\n// moved into this type.\ntype patcher struct {\n\t// Pieces of RequestScope\n\tnamer               ScopeNamer\n\tcreater             runtime.ObjectCreater\n\tdefaulter           runtime.ObjectDefaulter\n\ttyper               runtime.ObjectTyper\n\tunsafeConvertor     runtime.ObjectConvertor\n\tresource            schema.GroupVersionResource\n\tkind                schema.GroupVersionKind\n\tsubresource         string\n\tdryRun              bool\n\tvalidationDirective string\n\n\tobjectInterfaces admission.ObjectInterfaces\n\n\thubGroupVersion schema.GroupVersion\n\n\t// Validation functions\n\tcreateValidation rest.ValidateObjectFunc\n\tupdateValidation rest.ValidateObjectUpdateFunc\n\tadmissionCheck   admission.MutationInterface\n\n\tcodec runtime.Codec\n\n\toptions *metav1.PatchOptions\n\n\t// Operation information\n\trestPatcher rest.Patcher\n\tname        string\n\tpatchType   types.PatchType\n\tpatchBytes  []byte\n\tuserAgent   string\n\n\t// Set at invocation-time (by applyPatch) and immutable thereafter\n\tnamespace         string\n\tupdatedObjectInfo rest.UpdatedObjectInfo\n\tmechanism         patchMechanism\n\tforceAllowCreate  bool\n}\n\ntype patchMechanism interface {\n\tapplyPatchToCurrentObject(requextContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error)\n\tcreateNewObject(requestContext context.Context) (runtime.Object, error)\n}\n\ntype jsonPatcher struct {\n\t*patcher\n\n\tfieldManager *managedfields.FieldManager\n}\n\nfunc (p *jsonPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\t// Encode will convert & return a versioned object in JSON.\n\tcurrentObjJS, err := runtime.Encode(p.codec, currentObject)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// Apply the patch.\n\tpatchedObjJS, appliedStrictErrs, err := p.applyJSPatch(currentObjJS)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the resulting typed, unversioned object.\n\tobjToUpdate := p.restPatcher.New()\n\tif err := runtime.DecodeInto(p.codec, patchedObjJS, objToUpdate); err != nil {\n\t\tstrictError, isStrictError := runtime.AsStrictDecodingError(err)\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase !isStrictError:\n\t\t\t// disregard any appliedStrictErrs, because it's an incomplete\n\t\t\t// list of strict errors given that we don't know what fields were\n\t\t\t// unknown because DecodeInto failed. Non-strict errors trump in this case.\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), err.Error()),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn:\n\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, append(appliedStrictErrs, strictError.Errors()...))\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tstrictDecodingError := runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(append(appliedStrictErrs, strictError.Errors()...))\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), strictDecodingError.Error()),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t} else if len(appliedStrictErrs) > 0 {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn:\n\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, appliedStrictErrs)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewInvalid(schema.GroupKind{}, \"\", field.ErrorList{\n\t\t\t\tfield.Invalid(field.NewPath(\"patch\"), string(patchedObjJS), runtime.NewStrictDecodingError(appliedStrictErrs).Error()),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif p.options == nil {\n\t\t// Provide a more informative error for the crash that would\n\t\t// happen on the next line\n\t\tpanic(\"PatchOptions required but not provided\")\n\t}\n\tobjToUpdate = p.fieldManager.UpdateNoErrors(currentObject, objToUpdate, managerOrUserAgent(p.options.FieldManager, p.userAgent))\n\treturn objToUpdate, nil\n}\n\nfunc (p *jsonPatcher) createNewObject(_ context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name)\n}\n\ntype jsonPatchOp struct {\n\tOp    string      `json:\"op\"`\n\tPath  string      `json:\"path\"`\n\tFrom  string      `json:\"from\"`\n\tValue interface{} `json:\"value\"`\n}\n\n// applyJSPatch applies the patch. Input and output objects must both have\n// the external version, since that is what the patch must have been constructed against.\nfunc (p *jsonPatcher) applyJSPatch(versionedJS []byte) (patchedJS []byte, strictErrors []error, retErr error) {\n\tswitch p.patchType {\n\tcase types.JSONPatchType:\n\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n\t\t\tvar v []jsonPatchOp\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tif strictErrors, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(p.patchBytes, &v); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding patch: %v\", err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor i, e := range strictErrors {\n\t\t\t\tstrictErrors[i] = fmt.Errorf(\"json patch %v\", e)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tpatchObj, err := jsonpatch.DecodePatch(p.patchBytes)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(patchObj) > maxJSONPatchOperations {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewRequestEntityTooLargeError(\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"The allowed maximum operations in a JSON patch is %d, got %d\",\n\t\t\t\t\tmaxJSONPatchOperations, len(patchObj)))\n\t\t}\n\t\tpatchedJS, err := patchObj.Apply(versionedJS)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewGenericServerResponse(http.StatusUnprocessableEntity, \"\", schema.GroupResource{}, \"\", err.Error(), 0, false)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn patchedJS, strictErrors, nil\n\tcase types.MergePatchType:\n\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n\t\t\tv := map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tstrictErrors, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(p.patchBytes, &v)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding patch: %v\", err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tpatchedJS, retErr = jsonpatch.MergePatch(versionedJS, p.patchBytes)\n\t\tif retErr == jsonpatch.ErrBadJSONPatch {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, errors.NewBadRequest(retErr.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn patchedJS, strictErrors, retErr\n\tdefault:\n\t\t// only here as a safety net - go-restful filters content-type\n\t\treturn nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown Content-Type header for patch: %v\", p.patchType)\n\t}\n}\n\ntype smpPatcher struct {\n\t*patcher\n\n\t// Schema\n\tschemaReferenceObj runtime.Object\n\tfieldManager       *managedfields.FieldManager\n}\n\nfunc (p *smpPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\t// Since the patch is applied on versioned objects, we need to convert the\n\t// current object to versioned representation first.\n\tcurrentVersionedObject, err := p.unsafeConvertor.ConvertToVersion(currentObject, p.kind.GroupVersion())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tversionedObjToUpdate, err := p.creater.New(p.kind)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif err := strategicPatchObject(requestContext, p.defaulter, currentVersionedObject, p.patchBytes, versionedObjToUpdate, p.schemaReferenceObj, p.validationDirective); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\t// Convert the object back to the hub version\n\tnewObj, err := p.unsafeConvertor.ConvertToVersion(versionedObjToUpdate, p.hubGroupVersion)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tnewObj = p.fieldManager.UpdateNoErrors(currentObject, newObj, managerOrUserAgent(p.options.FieldManager, p.userAgent))\n\treturn newObj, nil\n}\n\nfunc (p *smpPatcher) createNewObject(_ context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name)\n}\n\nfunc newApplyPatcher(p *patcher, fieldManager *managedfields.FieldManager, unmarshalFn, unmarshalStrictFn func([]byte, interface{}) error) *applyPatcher {\n\treturn &applyPatcher{\n\t\tfieldManager:        fieldManager,\n\t\tpatch:               p.patchBytes,\n\t\toptions:             p.options,\n\t\tcreater:             p.creater,\n\t\tkind:                p.kind,\n\t\tuserAgent:           p.userAgent,\n\t\tvalidationDirective: p.validationDirective,\n\t\tunmarshalFn:         unmarshalFn,\n\t\tunmarshalStrictFn:   unmarshalStrictFn,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype applyPatcher struct {\n\tpatch               []byte\n\toptions             *metav1.PatchOptions\n\tcreater             runtime.ObjectCreater\n\tkind                schema.GroupVersionKind\n\tfieldManager        *managedfields.FieldManager\n\tuserAgent           string\n\tvalidationDirective string\n\tunmarshalFn         func(data []byte, v interface{}) error\n\tunmarshalStrictFn   func(data []byte, v interface{}) error\n}\n\nfunc (p *applyPatcher) applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext context.Context, obj runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\tforce := false\n\tif p.options.Force != nil {\n\t\tforce = *p.options.Force\n\t}\n\tif p.fieldManager == nil {\n\t\tpanic(\"FieldManager must be installed to run apply\")\n\t}\n\n\tpatchObj := &unstructured.Unstructured{Object: map[string]interface{}{}}\n\tif err := p.unmarshalFn(p.patch, &patchObj.Object); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error decoding YAML: %v\", err))\n\t}\n\n\tobj, err := p.fieldManager.Apply(obj, patchObj, p.options.FieldManager, force)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn obj, err\n\t}\n\n\t// TODO: spawn something to track deciding whether a fieldValidation=Strict\n\t// fatal error should return before an error from the apply operation\n\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict || p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn {\n\t\tif err := p.unmarshalStrictFn(p.patch, &map[string]interface{}{}); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif p.validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, errors.NewBadRequest(fmt.Sprintf(\"error strict decoding YAML: %v\", err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taddStrictDecodingWarnings(requestContext, []error{err})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn obj, nil\n}\n\nfunc (p *applyPatcher) createNewObject(requestContext context.Context) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\tobj, err := p.creater.New(p.kind)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create new object: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn p.applyPatchToCurrentObject(requestContext, obj)\n}\n\n// strategicPatchObject applies a strategic merge patch of `patchBytes` to\n// `originalObject` and stores the result in `objToUpdate`.\n// It additionally returns the map[string]interface{} representation of the\n// `originalObject` and `patchBytes`.\n// NOTE: Both `originalObject` and `objToUpdate` are supposed to be versioned.\nfunc strategicPatchObject(\n\trequestContext context.Context,\n\tdefaulter runtime.ObjectDefaulter,\n\toriginalObject runtime.Object,\n\tpatchBytes []byte,\n\tobjToUpdate runtime.Object,\n\tschemaReferenceObj runtime.Object,\n\tvalidationDirective string,\n) error {\n\toriginalObjMap, err := runtime.DefaultUnstructuredConverter.ToUnstructured(originalObject)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tpatchMap := make(map[string]interface{})\n\tvar strictErrs []error\n\tif validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationWarn || validationDirective == metav1.FieldValidationStrict {\n\t\tstrictErrs, err = kjson.UnmarshalStrict(patchBytes, &patchMap)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif err = kjson.UnmarshalCaseSensitivePreserveInts(patchBytes, &patchMap); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.NewBadRequest(err.Error())\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif err := applyPatchToObject(requestContext, defaulter, originalObjMap, patchMap, objToUpdate, schemaReferenceObj, strictErrs, validationDirective); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// applyPatch is called every time GuaranteedUpdate asks for the updated object,\n// and is given the currently persisted object as input.\n// TODO: rename this function because the name implies it is related to applyPatcher\nfunc (p *patcher) applyPatch(ctx context.Context, _, currentObject runtime.Object) (objToUpdate runtime.Object, patchErr error) {\n\t// Make sure we actually have a persisted currentObject\n\ttracing.SpanFromContext(ctx).AddEvent(\"About to apply patch\")\n\tcurrentObjectHasUID, err := hasUID(currentObject)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t} else if !currentObjectHasUID {\n\t\tobjToUpdate, patchErr = p.mechanism.createNewObject(ctx)\n\t} else {\n\t\tobjToUpdate, patchErr = p.mechanism.applyPatchToCurrentObject(ctx, currentObject)\n\t}\n\n\tif patchErr != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, patchErr\n\t}\n\n\tobjToUpdateHasUID, err := hasUID(objToUpdate)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif objToUpdateHasUID && !currentObjectHasUID {\n\t\taccessor, err := meta.Accessor(objToUpdate)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil, errors.NewConflict(p.resource.GroupResource(), p.name, fmt.Errorf(\"uid mismatch: the provided object specified uid %s, and no existing object was found\", accessor.GetUID()))\n\t}\n\n\t// if this object supports namespace info\n\tif objectMeta, err := meta.Accessor(objToUpdate); err == nil {\n\t\t// ensure namespace on the object is correct, or error if a conflicting namespace was set in the object\n\t\tif err := rest.EnsureObjectNamespaceMatchesRequestNamespace(rest.ExpectedNamespaceForResource(p.namespace, p.resource), objectMeta); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif err := checkName(objToUpdate, p.name, p.namespace, p.namer); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn objToUpdate, nil\n}\n\nfunc (p *patcher) admissionAttributes(ctx context.Context, updatedObject runtime.Object, currentObject runtime.Object, operation admission.Operation, operationOptions runtime.Object) admission.Attributes {\n\tuserInfo, _ := request.UserFrom(ctx)\n\treturn admission.NewAttributesRecord(updatedObject, currentObject, p.kind, p.namespace, p.name, p.resource, p.subresource, operation, operationOptions, p.dryRun, userInfo)\n}\n\n// applyAdmission is called every time GuaranteedUpdate asks for the updated object,\n// and is given the currently persisted object and the patched object as input.\n// TODO: rename this function because the name implies it is related to applyPatcher\nfunc (p *patcher) applyAdmission(ctx context.Context, patchedObject runtime.Object, currentObject runtime.Object) (runtime.Object, error) {\n\ttracing.SpanFromContext(ctx).AddEvent(\"About to check admission control\")\n\tvar operation admission.Operation\n\tvar options runtime.Object\n\tif hasUID, err := hasUID(currentObject); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t} else if !hasUID {\n\t\toperation = admission.Create\n\t\tcurrentObject = nil\n\t\toptions = patchToCreateOptions(p.options)\n\t} else {\n\t\toperation = admission.Update\n\t\toptions = patchToUpdateOptions(p.options)\n\t}\n\tif p.admissionCheck != nil && p.admissionCheck.Handles(operation) {\n\t\tattributes := p.admissionAttributes(ctx, patchedObject, currentObject, operation, options)\n\t\treturn patchedObject, p.admissionCheck.Admit(ctx, attributes, p.objectInterfaces)\n\t}\n\treturn patchedObject, nil\n}\n\n// patchResource divides PatchResource for easier unit testing\nfunc (p *patcher) patchResource(ctx context.Context, scope *RequestScope) (runtime.Object, bool, error) {\n\tp.namespace = request.NamespaceValue(ctx)\n\tswitch p.patchType {\n\tcase types.JSONPatchType, types.MergePatchType:\n\t\tp.mechanism = &jsonPatcher{\n\t\t\tpatcher:      p,\n\t\t\tfieldManager: scope.FieldManager,\n\t\t}\n\tcase types.StrategicMergePatchType:\n\t\tschemaReferenceObj, err := p.unsafeConvertor.ConvertToVersion(p.restPatcher.New(), p.kind.GroupVersion())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, false, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tp.mechanism = &smpPatcher{\n\t\t\tpatcher:            p,\n\t\t\tschemaReferenceObj: schemaReferenceObj,\n\t\t\tfieldManager:       scope.FieldManager,\n\t\t}\n\t// this case is unreachable if ServerSideApply is not enabled because we will have already rejected the content type\n\tcase types.ApplyYAMLPatchType:\n\t\tp.mechanism = newApplyPatcher(p, scope.FieldManager, yaml.Unmarshal, yaml.UnmarshalStrict)\n\t\tp.forceAllowCreate = true\n\tcase types.ApplyCBORPatchType:\n\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.CBORServingAndStorage) {\n\t\t\tutilruntime.HandleErrorWithContext(context.TODO(), nil, \"CBOR apply requests should be rejected before reaching this point unless the feature gate is enabled.\")\n\t\t\treturn nil, false, fmt.Errorf(\"%v: unimplemented patch type\", p.patchType)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// The strict and non-strict funcs are the same here because any CBOR map with\n\t\t// duplicate keys is invalid and always
